## ğŸ˜»âœ” å› å¼åˆ†è§£ 

å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ª `calc` æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å°†è¾“å…¥çš„æ•°æ‹†è§£ä¸ºå°½å¯èƒ½å¤šçš„ä¹˜æ•°ï¼Œæ‰€æœ‰æ•°ç›¸ä¹˜ç­‰äºè¾“å…¥æ•°ã€‚

```javascript
calc(2) // [2]
calc(8) // [2, 2, 2]
calc(24) // [2, 2, 2, 3]
calc(30) // [2, 3, 5]
```

```javascript
function calc(n) {
  const res = []
  let prev = n
  let i = 2

  while (i <= prev) {
    if (prev % i === 0) {
      res.push(i)
      prev /= i
      i = 2
    } else if (i < prev) {
      i++
    } else if (i === prev) {
      res.push(i)
    }
  }
  console.log(res)

  return res
}
```

# from - å…¶ä»–

## âœ” ä»æ•°ç»„ä¸­æ‰¾å‡ºå’Œä¸ºæŸä¸ªå€¼çš„ä¸¤æ•°ä¸‹æ ‡

> ç»™å®šä¸€ä¸ªæ•´æ•°æ•°ç»„ nums å’Œä¸€ä¸ªç›®æ ‡å€¼ targetï¼Œè¯·ä½ åœ¨è¯¥æ•°ç»„ä¸­æ‰¾å‡ºå’Œä¸ºç›®æ ‡å€¼çš„é‚£ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•´æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶è¿”å›ä»–ä»¬çš„æ•°ç»„ä¸‹æ ‡ã€‚ä½ å¯ä»¥å‡è®¾æ¯ç§è¾“å…¥åªä¼šå¯¹åº”ä¸€ä¸ªç­”æ¡ˆã€‚ä½†æ˜¯ï¼Œä½ ä¸èƒ½é‡å¤åˆ©ç”¨è¿™ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­åŒæ ·çš„å…ƒç´ ã€‚ ç¤ºä¾‹: ç»™å®š nums = [2, 7, 11, 15], target = 9 å› ä¸º nums[0] + nums[1] = 2 + 7 = 9 æ‰€ä»¥è¿”å› [0, 1]ã€‚

åˆå§‹ä»£ç ï¼š

```javascript
const twoSum = (nums, target) => {}
```

---

è§£æ³• 1 - `Map`ï¼š

```javascript
const twoSum = (nums, target) => {
  const map = new Map()
  for (let i = 0, len = nums.length; i < len; i++) {
    if (map.get(nums[i])) {
      return [map.get(nums[i]), i]
    }
    map.set(target - nums[i], i)
  }
}
```

è§£æ³• 2 - ä¸¤æ¬¡å¾ªç¯ï¼š

```javascript
const twoSum = (nums, target) => {
  for (let i = 0, len = nums.length; i < len; i++) {
    for (let j = i + 1; j < len; j++) {
      if (nums[i] + nums[j] === target) return [i, j]
    }
  }
}
```

# leetcode åˆ·é¢˜è®°å½•

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 1 ä¸¤æ•°ä¹‹å’Œã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/two-sum/)

Mapã€å­—å…¸

```js
var twoSum = function (nums, target) {
  // for (var i = 0; i < nums.length; i++) {
  //   for (var j = i + 1; j < nums.length; j++) {
  //     if (nums[i] + nums[j] === target) return [i, j]
  //   }
  // }
  const m = new Map()
  for (let i = 0; i < nums.length; i++) {
    const num = nums[i]
    const other = target - num
    if (m.has(other)) {
      return [m.get(other), i]
    } else {
      m.set(num, i)
    }
  }
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 2 ä¸¤æ•°ç›¸åŠ ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/add-two-numbers/)

é“¾è¡¨

```js
var addTwoNumbers = function (l1, l2) {
  const head = new ListNode()
  let curr = head
  let add = 0
  let sum = 0
  while (l1 || l2) {
    sum = (l1 ? l1.val : 0) + (l2 ? l2.val : 0) + add
    add = Math.floor(sum / 10)
    curr.next = new ListNode(sum - 10 * add)
    l1 = l1 && l1.next
    l2 = l2 && l2.next
    curr = curr.next
  }
  if (add > 0) {
    curr.next = new ListNode(1)
  }

  return head.next
}

function ListNode(val, next) {
  this.val = val === undefined ? 0 : val
  this.next = next === undefined ? null : next
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 3 æ— é‡å¤å­—ç¬¦çš„æœ€é•¿å­ä¸²ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/longest-substring-without-repeating-characters/)

æ»‘åŠ¨çª—å£ã€å­—å…¸

```js
var lengthOfLongestSubstring = function(s) {
  let max = 0
  const set = new Set()
  let i=0
  for(let j=0;j<s.length;j++) {
    while(set.has(s[j])) {
      set.delete(s[i])
      i++
    }
    set.add(s[j])
    max = Math.max(max, set.size)
  }
  return max
};
```

```js
var lengthOfLongestSubstring = function (s) {
  let maxLen = 0
  let currStr = ''
  for (let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
    const indInCurrStr = currStr.indexOf(s[i])
    let len
    if (indInCurrStr === -1) {
      currStr += s[i]
      len = currStr.length
    } else {
      len = currStr.length
      currStr = currStr.slice(indInCurrStr + 1) + s[i]
    }
    maxLen = len > maxLen ? len : maxLen
  }
  return maxLen
}
```

or

```js
var lengthOfLongestSubstring = function (s) {
  let l = 0
  let max = 0
  const m = new Map()
  for (let r = 0; r < s.length; r++) {
    if (m.has(s[r]) && m.get(s[r]) >= l) {
      l = m.get(s[r]) + 1
    }
    m.set(s[r], r)
    max = Math.max(max, r - l + 1)
  }
  return max
}
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 4 å¯»æ‰¾ä¸¤ä¸ªæ­£åºæ•°ç»„çš„ä¸­ä½æ•°ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/median-of-two-sorted-arrays/)

äºŒåˆ†æŸ¥æ‰¾

```js

// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(log(m + n))
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var findMedianSortedArrays = function(nums1, nums2) {
  // åˆ©ç”¨ä¸­ä½æ•°çš„ç‰¹æ®Šå±æ€§
  const m = nums1.length
  const n = nums2.length
  const totalLength = m + n
  if(totalLength % 2 === 1) {
    // ä¸­ä½æ•°å°±åœ¨æ•°ç»„ä¸­
    const mid = (totalLength - 1) / 2
    return getTarget(mid + 1, nums1, nums2)
  } else {
    // ä¸­ä½æ•°æ˜¯æœ€ä¸­é—´ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°çš„å‡å€¼
    const mid = totalLength / 2
    return (getTarget(mid, nums1, nums2) + getTarget(mid + 1, nums1, nums2)) / 2
  }
};

// è½¬åŒ–ä¸ºè·å– nums1 å’Œ nums2 æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„ç¬¬ k å¤§çš„æ•°
// ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç»„æ˜¯æ’å¥½åºçš„æ•°ç»„
function getTarget(k, nums1, nums2) {
  // å¯¹äºä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­ä¸‹æ ‡ä¸º k / 2 - 1(å³ç¬¬ k / 2 ä¸ª) çš„æ•°å­—A(k / 2 - 1)å’Œ B(k / 2 - 1)
  // ----------------------------------------------------------------------
  // å¦‚æœ A(k / 2 - 1) < B(k / 2 - 1) ï¼Œåˆ™æœ‰è¿™æ ·ä¸€ä¸ªè§„åˆ™å­˜åœ¨
  // åœ¨ Aã€B ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç»„çš„å‰ k / 2 ä¸ªæ•°å­—ä¸­ï¼ˆå³ A+B çš„å‰Kä¸ªæ•°å­—ä¸­ï¼‰ï¼ŒA(k / 2 - 1)æœ€å¤šåªèƒ½æ˜¯ç¬¬ k - 1 ä¸ªæ•°å­—ï¼Œä¸å¯èƒ½æ˜¯ç¬¬ K ä¸ªæ•°å­—
  // ç”±äº A(k / 2 - 1)  å‰é¢çš„æ•°å­—æ¯”å®ƒè¿˜å°ï¼Œåˆ™å…¶å‰é¢çš„æ•°å­—åªèƒ½æ’åœ¨A + B æ•°ç»„çš„ k - 1 ä¹‹å‰ï¼Œåˆ™å¯ä»¥æ–­å®šï¼Œç¬¬ K ä¸ªæ•°å­—è‚¯å®šä¸åœ¨ A[0]~A[k / 2 - 1] å†…
  // å°±å¯ä»¥æŠŠ A ä¸­ä¸‹æ ‡åœ¨ k / 2 ä¹‹å‰çš„å…¨éƒ¨æ’é™¤
  // æ’é™¤ä¹‹åï¼Œæ–°çš„ newK = k - (k / 2)
  // ----------------------------------------------------------------------
  // å¦‚æœ A(k / 2 - 1) > B(k / 2 - 1) åˆ™å¯¹ B è¿›è¡Œä¸Šé¢çš„æ“ä½œ
  // ----------------------------------------------------------------------
  // å¦‚æœ A(k / 2 - 1) === B(k / 2 - 1) ï¼Œåˆ™ A ä¸­ k / 2 - 1 å‰é¢çš„æ•°å­—å’Œ B ä¸­ k / 2 - 1 å‰é¢çš„æ•°å­—åˆå¹¶èµ·æ¥ï¼Œä¹Ÿæœ€å¤šåªèƒ½æ’åœ¨ k - 2 ä½
  // åˆ™å®é™…ä¸Š A(k / 2 - 1) å’Œ B(k / 2 - 1) å‰é¢çš„æ•°å­—éƒ½å¯ä»¥ã€æ’é™¤æ‰ã€‘
  // å› ä¸º A(k / 2 - 1) å’Œ B(k / 2 - 1) æ˜¯ç›¸ç­‰çš„ï¼Œåˆ™ A(k / 2 - 1) è¿™ä¸€é¡¹ä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥æ’é™¤æ‰ï¼Œæç«¯æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œåˆšå¥½ B(k / 2 - 1) å°±æ˜¯æƒ³è¦çš„å€¼
  // ç»¼åˆä¹‹åå°±æ˜¯ï¼Œä¸¤è€…ç›¸ç­‰çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œé€‰æ‹©åŒ A(k / 2 - 1) < B(k / 2 - 1) ä¸€æ ·çš„æ“ä½œï¼ŒæŠŠ A ä¸­å‰ k / 2 ä¸ªæ•°å­—å…¨éƒ¨æ’é™¤æ‰
  // ----------------------------------------------------------------------
  // ç”±äº k è¡¨ç¤ºçš„æ˜¯åœ¨ å‰©ä¸‹çš„ nums1 å’Œ nums2 åˆå¹¶åçš„æœ‰åºæ•°ç»„ä¸­ï¼Œç¬¬ k ä¸ªæ•°å­—
  // åˆ™å½“ k = 1 çš„æ—¶å€™ ï¼Œç›´æ¥æ¯”è¾ƒå‰©ä¸‹çš„ nums1 å’Œ nums2 ä¸¤æ•°ç»„ä¸­é åœ¨æœ€å‰é¢ä¸”æœªè¢«æ’é™¤çš„ä¸‹æ ‡ï¼Œå³å¯å¾—å‡ºç»“æœã€‚
  // ----------------------------------------------------------------------
  // è¿™é‡Œ k å¯èƒ½æ˜¯å¥‡æ•°ä¹Ÿå¯èƒ½æ˜¯å¶æ•°ï¼Œæ˜¯å¶æ•°å°±å®Œå…¨ç¬¦åˆä¸Šé¢çš„æ¨æ–­ï¼Œæ˜¯å¥‡æ•°çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œ k / 2 å‘ä¸‹å–æ•´
  // è¿™æ · Math.floor(k / 2) * 2 < kï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ä»ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸Šå–çš„æ•°ä¹‹å’Œå°äº k
  // å½“ A(Math.floor(k / 2) - 1) < B(Math.floor(k / 2) - 1) æˆç«‹çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼ŒA(Math.floor(k / 2) - 1) æœ€å¤šåªèƒ½æ’åœ¨ç¬¬ Math.floor(k / 2) * 2 - 1 çš„ä½ç½®ä¸Š
  // Math.floor(k / 2) * 2 - 1 < k - 1ï¼Œæ•… A(Math.floor(k / 2) - 1) å¯¹åº”çš„æ•°å­—åŠå…¶å‰é¢çš„æ•°å­—éƒ½èƒ½æ’é™¤æ‰ï¼Œè¿™å’Œ k æ˜¯å¶æ•°çš„æ—¶å€™å®Œå…¨ä¸€æ ·
  // å½“ A(Math.floor(k / 2) - 1) === B(Math.floor(k / 2) - 1) æˆç«‹çš„æ—¶å€™
  // A(Math.floor(k / 2) - 1) æœ€å¤šæ’åœ¨ç¬¬ Math.floor(k / 2) * 2 çš„ä½ç½®ï¼Œè€Œ Math.floor(k / 2) * 2 < kï¼Œæ•…ç»“æœ k æ˜¯å¶æ•°çš„æ—¶å€™ä¹Ÿæ˜¯ä¸€è‡´çš„
  // ----------------------------------------------------------------------
  // ä¸Šè¿°æ€è·¯å¯¹åº”çš„æ˜¯ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­å­˜åœ¨æ•°å­—å¤§äºä¸­ä½æ•°ï¼Œåˆ™ä¸€ç›´æ‰§è¡Œä¸Šè¿°æ“ä½œç›´åˆ°è·å–åˆ°ç¬¬kä¸ªæ•°æ•°å­—çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­éƒ½è¿˜æœ‰æ•°å­—
  // è¿˜æœ‰å¦å¤–ä¸€ç§æƒ…å†µï¼ŒæŸä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„æ•°å­—å…¨éƒ¨æ’åœ¨ä¸­ä½æ•°å‰é¢
  // åˆ™è‚¯å®šä¼šå‡ºç°ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„æ‰€æœ‰æ•°å­—å…¨éƒ¨æ˜¯ä¸éœ€è¦çš„æ•°å­—
  // å½“ä¸Šè¿°æ“ä½œæ‰§è¡Œåˆ°æŸä¸ªæ•°ç»„çš„ä¸‹æ ‡è¶…è¿‡è¾¹ç•Œçš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œåªéœ€è¦åœ¨å¦ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­æ‰¾åˆ°ç¬¬ kï¼ˆå»æ‰è¢«æ’é™¤çš„æ•°å­—ï¼‰ ä¸ªæ•°å­—å³æ˜¯ç»“æœ

  let nums1Target
  let nums2Target
  let halfK
  let showDropCount
  let ind1 = 0
  let ind2 = 0

  while(true) {
    if(ind1 >= nums1.length) {
      return nums2[ind2 + k - 1]
    }
    if(ind2 >= nums2.length) {
      return nums1[ind1 + k - 1]
    }
    if(k === 1) {
      return Math.min(nums1[ind1], nums2[ind2])
    }
    halfK = Math.floor(k / 2)
    // showDropCount è¡¨ç¤ºåº”è¯¥ä¸¢å¼ƒçš„æ•°å­—ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œç”±äºå¯èƒ½å­˜åœ¨ä¸‹æ ‡è¶Šç•Œçš„é—®é¢˜ï¼Œå½“ä¸‹æ ‡è¶Šç•Œå‡ºç°çš„æ—¶å€™
    // é»˜è®¤ä½¿ç”¨æ•°ç»„çš„æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—æ¥åšæ¯”è¾ƒï¼Œè€Œè¿™ä¸ªæ—¶å€™è¦æ’é™¤çš„æ•°å­—ä¸ªæ•°å°±å¯èƒ½ä¸æ˜¯ halfK ä¸ªäº†
    showDropCount = halfK
    // è¶…å‡ºäº†æ•°ç»„é•¿åº¦ï¼Œåˆ™ä½¿ç”¨æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯æ•°ç»„ä¸­æœ€å¤§çš„ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°
    if(ind1 + halfK - 1 >= nums1.length) {
      nums1Target = nums1[nums1.length - 1]
      showDropCount = nums1.length  - ind1
    } else {
      nums1Target = nums1[ind1 + halfK - 1]
    }
    if(ind2 + halfK - 1 >= nums2.length) {
      nums2Target = nums2[nums2.length - 1]
      showDropCount = nums2.length - ind2
    } else {
      nums2Target = nums2[ind2 + halfK - 1]
    }

    if(nums1Target <= nums2Target) {
      ind1 = ind1 + showDropCount
    } else {
      ind2 = ind2 + showDropCount
    }

    k = k - showDropCount
  }
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 5 æœ€é•¿å›æ–‡å­ä¸²ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/longest-palindromic-substring/submissions/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
var longestPalindrome = function(s) {
  const len = s.length
  let maxStr = s[0]
  const dp = new Array(len).fill(false).map(_ => new Array(len).fill(false))

  for(let i=0;i<len;i++) {
    dp[i][i] = true
  }

  for(let L=2;L<=len;L++) {
    for(let i=0;i + L - 1 <len;i++) {
      if(s[i] === s[i + L - 1]) {
        dp[i][i + L - 1] = i + L - 2 >= i + 1 ? dp[i + 1][i + L - 2] : true
        if(dp[i][i + L - 1] && L > maxStr.length) {
          maxStr = s.slice(i, i + L)
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return maxStr
};
```

å¸¸è§„ä¸­å¿ƒå¾€ä¸¤ä¾§æ‰©æ•£

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var longestPalindrome = function(s) {
  let maxStr = ''
  for(let i=0;i<s.length;i++) {
    // æ‰«æä¸¤æ¬¡
    // å•ä¸­å¿ƒæ‰«æ
    let l=r=i
    while(r + 1 < s.length && l - 1 >= 0 && s[r + 1] === s[l - 1]) {
      l--
      r++
    }
    if(maxStr.length < r - l + 1) {
      maxStr = s.slice(l, r + 1)
    }
    // åŒä¸­å¿ƒæ‰«æ
    if(i + 1 < s.length && s[i] === s[i + 1]) {
      l = i
      r = i + 1
      while(r + 1 < s.length && l - 1 >= 0 && s[r + 1] === s[l - 1]) {
        l--
        r++
      }
      if(maxStr.length < r - l + 1) {
        maxStr = s.slice(l, r + 1)
      }
    }

  }
  return maxStr
};
```

è´ªå¿ƒç®—æ³•

æ ¸å¿ƒå°±æ˜¯å°è¯•ä»¥æ¯ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸ºä¸­å¿ƒï¼Œå¾€ä¸¤ä¾§æ‰©æ•£

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(0^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var longestPalindrome = function(s) {
  let res = ''
  for(let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
    let end = findDuplicate(s, i)
    let l, r
    l = i - 1
    if(end === i + 1) {
      // ä¸­å¿ƒä¸æ˜¯é‡å¤å€¼
      r = i + 1
    } else {
      // ä¸­å¿ƒæ˜¯é‡å¤å€¼
      r = end
      // å› ä¸ºéƒ½æ˜¯é‡å¤å€¼ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ç›´æ¥æŠŠæ‰€æœ‰é‡å¤çš„å€¼éƒ½è·³è¿‡
      i = end - 1
    }
    while(l >= 0 && r < s.length && s[l] === s[r]) {
      l--
      r++
    }
    if(r - l - 1 > res.length) {
      res = s.slice(l + 1, r)
    }
  }
  return res
};


function findDuplicate(s, i) {
  let r = i
  while(s[i] === s[r]) {
    r++
  }
  return r
}
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 6 Z å­—å½¢å˜æ¢ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/zigzag-conversion/)


```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(k) k=numRows
var convert = function(s, numRows) {
  // è¡Œæ•°ä¸º 1 åˆ™ç›´æ¥è¿”å› s
  if(numRows === 1) return s
  // å»ºä¸€ä¸ª é•¿åº¦ä¸º numRows çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼Œæ•°ç»„ä¸­æ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ä¸ºç©ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
  // ä¸€ä¸ªç©ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¯¹åº”ç»“æœä¸­çš„ä¸€è¡Œ
  const resArr = new Array(numRows).fill('')
  // å¯¹æ¯ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ï¼Œè®¡ç®—å‡ºå…¶æ‰€å¤„çš„è¡Œ
  for(let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
    // 2 * numRows - 2 æœ€å°çš„ä¸€ä¸ªæ’åˆ—æ¥å›
    const m = i % (2 * numRows - 2)
    if(m <= numRows - 1) {
      // ä»ä¸Šå¾€ä¸‹
      resArr[m] += s[i]
    } else {
      // ä»ä¸‹å¾€ä¸Š
      const n = m - (numRows - 1)
      resArr[numRows - 1 - n] += s[i]
    }
  }
  return resArr.join('')
};
```


## ğŸ˜»âœ” 7 æ•´æ•°åè½¬ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/reverse-integer/)

```js
var reverse = function(x) {
  if(x === 0) return 0
  let isNegative = x < 0 ? true : false
  x = isNegative ? -x : x
  let result = 0
  while(x > 0) {
    const n = x % 10
    if(result > (2 ** 31 - 1 - n) / 10) return 0
    x = Math.floor(x / 10)
    result = 10 * result + n
  }
  return isNegative? -result : result
};
```

## ?? ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 8 å­—ç¬¦ä¸²è½¬æ¢æ•´æ•° (atoi)ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/string-to-integer-atoi/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var myAtoi = function(s) {
  while(s[0] === ' ') {
    s = s.slice(1)
  }
  let isNegative = false
  if(s[0] === '-') {
    isNegative = true
    s = s.slice(1)
  }else if(s[0] === '+') {
    s = s.slice(1)
  }
  let num = 0
  let i = 0
  while(i < s.length && s[i] >= '0' && s[i] <= '9') {
    if(!isNegative && (10 * num + Number(s[i]) > 2 ** 31 - 1)) {
      return 2 ** 31 - 1
    }else if(isNegative && (10 * num + Number(s[i]) > 2 ** 31 )) {
      return - (2 ** 31)
    }
    num = 10 * num + Number(s[i])
    i++
  }
  return !isNegative ? num : -num
};
```


## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 9 å›æ–‡æ•°ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/palindrome-number/)

å¯¹å›æ–‡æ•°æ¯”è¾ƒå¥½çš„è§£å†³åŠæ³•æ˜¯ï¼ŒæŠŠä»æ•°å­—ä¸­å–åˆ°çš„ä½™æ•°å…¨éƒ¨å­˜è¿›æ•°ç»„ä¸­ï¼Œè¿™æ ·å°±ç®—æ˜¯0ä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥è¡¨ç¤ºï¼Œå¦‚æœæ˜¯ç›´æ¥è®¡ç®—æˆæ•°å­—åˆ™å¯èƒ½å‡ºç° 00123 è¿™ç§æƒ…å†µï¼Œè€Œå‰å¯¼0ä¼šè¢«çœç•¥ï¼Œå¯¼è‡´å‡ºé”™ã€‚

```js
var isPalindrome = function(x) {
  if(x < 0) return false
  if(x === 0) return true
  let nums = []
  while(x > 0) {
    nums.push(x % 10)
    x = Math.floor(x / 10)
  }
  for(let i=0;i<nums.length / 2;i++) {
    if(nums[i] !== nums[nums.length - 1 - i]) {
      return false
    }
  }
  return true
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 10 æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼åŒ¹é…ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/regular-expression-matching/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
var isMatch = function(s, p) {
  const m = s.length
  const n = p.length
  const dp = new Array(m + 1).fill(false).map(_ => new Array(n + 1).fill(false))
  dp[0][0] = true
  for(let j=2;j<=n;j+=2) {
    if(p[j - 1] === '*') {
      dp[0][j] = dp[0][j - 2]
    }
  }
  for(let i=1;i<=m;i++) {
    for(let j=1;j<=n;j++) {
      if(s[i - 1] === p[j - 1] || p[j - 1] === '.') {
        dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j - 1]
      } else if (p[j - 1] === '*') {
        dp[i][j] = dp[i][j-2] || false
        if(p[j - 2] === s[i - 1] || p[j - 2] === '.') {
          dp[i][j] = dp[i][j] || dp[i-1][j]
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return dp[m][n]
};

```

## ??ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 11 ç››æœ€å¤šæ°´çš„å®¹å™¨ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/container-with-most-water/)

åŒæŒ‡é’ˆ

[æˆ‘çš„é¢˜è§£](https://leetcode.cn/problems/container-with-most-water/solution/by-lxfriday-udsc/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var maxArea = function(height) {
  let l = 0
  let r = height.length - 1
  let max = 0
  while(l < r) {
    max = Math.max(Math.min(height[l], height[r]) * (r - l), max)
    if(height[l] <= height[r]) {
      l++
    } else {
      r--
    }
  }
  return max
}; 
```

## âœ” 13 ç½—é©¬æ•°å­—è½¬æ•´æ•°ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/roman-to-integer/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var romanToInt = function(s) {
  const map = {
    'I': 1,
    'V': 5,
    'X': 10,
    'L': 50,
    'C': 100,
    'D': 500,
    'M': 1000,
  }
  let sum = 0
  for(let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
    if(
      (s[i] === 'I' && (s[i + 1] === 'V' || s[i + 1] === 'X')) || 
      (s[i] === 'X' && (s[i + 1] === 'L' || s[i + 1] === 'C')) || 
      (s[i] === 'C' && (s[i + 1] === 'D' || s[i + 1] === 'M'))
    ) {
      sum -= map[s[i]]
    } else {
      sum += map[s[i]]
    }
  }
  return sum
};
```

## âœ” 14 æœ€é•¿å…¬å…±å‰ç¼€ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/longest-common-prefix/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n*k) k å…¬å…±å‰ç¼€çš„é•¿åº¦
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1) 
var longestCommonPrefix = function(strs) {
  for(let i = 0;i <= strs[0].length; i++) {
    const target = strs[0].slice(0, i)
    for(let j = 1; j < strs.length; j++) {
      if(strs[j].indexOf(target) !== 0) {
        return strs[0].slice(0, i - 1)
      }
    }
  }
  return strs[0]
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 15 ä¸‰æ•°ä¹‹å’Œ ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/3sum/)

åŒæŒ‡é’ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(logN) æ’åºçš„ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦
var threeSum = function(nums) {
  if(nums.length < 3) return []
  const res = []
  nums.sort((a, b) => a - b)
  const len = nums.length
  for(let i = 0; i < len - 2; i++) {
    if(nums[i] === nums[i - 1]) continue
    let l = i + 1
    let r = len - 1
    while(l < r) {
      if(l > i + 1 && nums[l] === nums[l - 1]) {
        l++
        continue
      }
      if(r < len - 1 && nums[r] === nums[r + 1]) {
        r--
        continue
      }
      const sum = nums[i] + nums[l] + nums[r]
      if(sum === 0) {
        res.push([nums[i], nums[l], nums[r]])
        l++
        r--
      } else if(sum > 0) {
        // åœ¨æ¯ä¸€ä¸ªè½®æ¬¡ä¸­ nums[i] å›ºå®šä¸å˜ï¼Œä¸”çŸ¥é“ nums[l] <= nums[r]
        // sum > 0 åˆ™ä¸‰ä¸ªæ•°ä¸­æœ€å¤§çš„æ•° nums[r] ä¸€å®šå¤§äº†ï¼Œ è¦å¾€å·¦ç§»
        // sum < 0 åˆ™ sum[l] å°äº†ï¼Œè¦å˜å¤§
        r--
      } else {
        l++
      }
    }
  }
  return res
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 16 æœ€æ¥è¿‘çš„ä¸‰æ•°ä¹‹å’Œã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/3sum-closest/)

åŒæŒ‡é’ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(logn) æ’åº
var threeSumClosest = function(nums, target) {
  nums.sort((a, b) => a - b)
  let finalSum
  let minGap = Infinity
  const len = nums.length
  for(let i=0;i<len;i++) {
    let l = i + 1
    let r = len - 1
    while(l < r) {
      const sum = nums[i] + nums[l] + nums[r]
      const gap = Math.abs(sum - target)
      if(gap < minGap) {
        finalSum = sum
        minGap = gap
      }
      (sum < target) ? (l++) : (r--)
    }
  }
  return finalSum
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 17. ç”µè¯å·ç çš„å­—æ¯ç»„åˆã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/letter-combinations-of-a-phone-number/)

å›æº¯ã€é€’å½’ã€æ’åˆ—ç»„åˆ

```js
// å›æº¯
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(3^M*4^N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(M+N)
var letterCombinations = function(digits) {
  if(!digits.length) return []
  const numMap = {
    2: ['a', 'b', 'c'],
    3: ['d', 'e', 'f'],
    4: ['g', 'h', 'i'],
    5: ['j', 'k', 'l'],
    6: ['m', 'n', 'o'],
    7: ['p', 'q', 'r', 's'],
    8: ['t', 'u', 'v'],
    9: ['w', 'x', 'y', 'z'],
  }
  const words = []
  for(let i=0;i<digits.length;i++) {
    words.push(numMap[digits[i]])
  }
  const len = words.length
  const res = []
  function dfs(path, startIndex) {
    if(path.length === len) {
      res.push(path)
      return
    } else {
      for(let word of words[startIndex]) {
        dfs(path + word, startIndex + 1)
      }
    }
  }
  dfs('', 0)
  return res
};

// [['a', 'b', 'c'], ['g', 'h', 'i'], ]
// [['a', 'b', 'c'], ['g', 'h', 'i'], ['g', 'h', 'i']]
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 18 å››æ•°ä¹‹å’Œã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/4sum/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^3)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(logN)
var fourSum = function(nums, target) {
  if(nums.length < 4) return []
  nums.sort((a, b) => a - b)
  const n = nums.length
  const res = []
  for(let i = 0;i<n - 3;i++) {
    if(i - 1 >= 0 && nums[i] === nums[i - 1]) continue
    const a = nums[i]
    const atarget = target - a
    for(let ii = i + 1;ii<n - 2;ii++) {
      if(ii - 1 >= i + 1 && nums[ii] === nums[ii - 1]) continue
      let b = nums[ii]
      let l = ii + 1, r = n - 1
      while(l < r) {
        const s = b + nums[l] + nums[r]
        if(s === atarget) {
          res.push([a, b, nums[l], nums[r]])
          while(nums[l] === nums[l + 1] && l < r) {
            l++
          }
          while(nums[r] === nums[r - 1] && l < r) {
            r--
          }
          l++
          r--
        } else {
          if(s > atarget) {
            r--
          } else {
            l++
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return res
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 20 æœ‰æ•ˆçš„æ‹¬å·ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/valid-parentheses/)

å…³é”®è¯ï¼šæ ˆ

```js
/**
 * @param {string} s
 * @return {boolean}
 */
var isValid = function (s) {
  const leftValues = '({['
  const map = {
    '(': ')',
    '{': '}',
    '[': ']',
  }
  const stack = []
  for (let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
    if (leftValues.includes(s[i])) {
      stack.push(s[i])
    } else {
      const lastValue = stack.pop()
      if (map[lastValue] !== s[i]) return false
    }
  }
  return !stack.length
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 21 åˆå¹¶ä¸¤ä¸ªæœ‰åºé“¾è¡¨ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/merge-two-sorted-lists/)

é“¾è¡¨

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n) n=list1.length + list2.length
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var mergeTwoLists = function(list1, list2) {
  const head = new ListNode()
  let th = head
  while(list1 && list2) {
    if(list1.val < list2.val) {
      th.next = list1
      list1 = list1.next
    } else {
      th.next = list2
      list2 = list2.next
    }
    th = th.next
  }
  if(list1) {
    th.next = list1
  }
  if(list2) {
    th.next = list2
  }
  return head.next
};
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 22 æ‹¬å·ç”Ÿæˆã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/generate-parentheses/)

å›æº¯ã€é€’å½’

```js
var generateParenthesis = function(n) {
  const res = []
  let leftCount = 0
  let rightCount = 0
  function calc(str) {
    if(leftCount < rightCount || leftCount > n || rightCount > n) return
    if(leftCount === n && rightCount === n) {
      res.push(str)
      return
    }
    leftCount++
    calc(str + '(')
    leftCount--
    rightCount++
    calc(str + ')')
    rightCount--
  }
  calc('')
  return res
};
```

## ?ğŸ˜»âœ” 23 åˆå¹¶Kä¸ªå‡åºé“¾è¡¨ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/merge-k-sorted-lists/)

é“¾è¡¨ã€å †ã€åˆ†æ²»æ³•ã€å½’å¹¶

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(kn*logk)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(logk)
var mergeKLists = function(lists, l, r) {
  l = typeof l === 'number' ? l : 0
  r = typeof r === 'number' ? r: lists.length - 1
  if(l === r) return lists[l]
  if(l > r) return null
  const mid = Math.floor((l + r) / 2)
  return merge(mergeKLists(lists, l, mid), mergeKLists(lists, mid + 1, r))
};

function merge(list1, list2) {
  const head = new ListNode()
  let tHead = head
  while(list1 && list2) {
    if(list1.val < list2.val) {
      tHead.next = list1
      list1 = list1.next
    } else {
      tHead.next = list2
      list2 = list2.next
    }
    tHead = tHead.next
  }
  if(list1) {
    tHead.next = list1
  }
  if(list2) {
    tHead.next = list2
  }
  return head.next
}
```

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(kn*logk)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(k)
// k æ˜¯ list.lenght
// n æ˜¯æ‰€æœ‰é“¾è¡¨èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„ä¸ªæ•°
var mergeKLists = function(lists) {
  const head = new ListNode()
  let th = head
  const h = new MinHeap()
  for(let list of lists) {
    list && h.insert(list)
  }

  while(h.size()) {
    let hPop = h.pop()
    th.next = hPop
    th = th.next
    if(hPop.next) h.insert(hPop.next)
  }

  return head.next
};
class MinHeap {
  constructor() {
    this.heap = []
  }

  insert(num) {
    this.heap.push(num)
    this.shiftUp(this.heap.length - 1)
  }

  pop() {
    this.swap(0, this.heap.length - 1)
    let p = this.heap.pop()
    this.shiftDown(0)
    return p
  }

  peek() {
    return this.heap[0]
  }

  size() {
    return this.heap.length
  }

  shiftDown(i) {
    const left = this.getLeftIndex(i)
    const right = this.getRightIndex(i)
    if (left < this.heap.length && this.heap[i].val > this.heap[left].val) {
      this.swap(i, left)
      this.shiftDown(left)
    }
    if (right < this.heap.length && this.heap[i].val > this.heap[right].val) {
      this.swap(i, right)
      this.shiftDown(right)
    }
  }

  shiftUp(i) {
    if (i === 0) return
    const parentIndex = this.getParentIndex(i)
    if (this.heap[parentIndex].val > this.heap[i].val) {
      this.swap(parentIndex, i)
      this.shiftUp(parentIndex)
    }
  }

  swap(i, j) {
    const t = this.heap[i]
    this.heap[i] = this.heap[j]
    this.heap[j] = t
  }

  getParentIndex(i) {
    return Math.floor((i - 1) / 2)
  }
  getLeftIndex(i) {
    return 2 * i + 1
  }
  getRightIndex(i) {
    return 2 * i + 2
  }
}
```

å¸¸è§„é¡ºåºåˆå¹¶

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n*k^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var mergeKLists = function(lists) {
  if(!lists.length) return null
  const len = lists.length
  const head = new ListNode()
  head.next = lists[0]
  for(let i=1;i<len;i++) {
    head.next = merge(head.next, lists[i])
  }
  return head.next
};

function merge(list1, list2) {
  const head = new ListNode()
  let tHead = head
  while(list1 && list2) {
    if(list1.val < list2.val) {
      tHead.next = list1
      list1 = list1.next
    } else {
      tHead.next = list2
      list2 = list2.next
    }
    tHead = tHead.next
  }
  if(list1) {
    tHead.next = list1
  }
  if(list2) {
    tHead.next = list2
  }
  return head.next
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 24 ä¸¤ä¸¤äº¤æ¢é“¾è¡¨ä¸­çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/swap-nodes-in-pairs/)

```js
var swapPairs = function(head) {
  let tHead = new ListNode()
  tHead.next = head
  let slow = tHead
  let fast = tHead
  while(fast.next && fast.next.next) {
    const tPrevSlow = slow
    slow = slow.next
    fast = fast.next.next
    const tFastNext = fast.next
    tPrevSlow.next = fast
    fast.next = slow
    slow.next = tFastNext
    fast = slow
  }
  return tHead.next
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 25 K ä¸ªä¸€ç»„ç¿»è½¬é“¾è¡¨ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/reverse-nodes-in-k-group/)

```js
// æ¯”è¾ƒä¼˜ç§€çš„ç‰ˆæœ¬
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var reverseKGroup = function(head, k) {
  let count = 0
  const myHead = new ListNode()
  myHead.next = head
  let start = myHead
  let end = start

  while(end.next) {
    end = end.next
    count++
    if(count % k === 0) {
      start = reverse(start, end)
      end = start
    }
  }
  return myHead.next
};

// start çš„ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹æ‰æ˜¯èµ·ç‚¹
// è¿”å›åè½¬åçš„ end èŠ‚ç‚¹
function reverse(start, end) {
  const myHead = new ListNode()
  const reversePrev = start
  const reverseNext = end.next
  start = start.next
  const prevStart = start
  while(myHead.next !== end) {
    const prev = myHead.next
    myHead.next = start
    start = start.next
    myHead.next.next = prev
  }
  reversePrev.next = myHead.next
  prevStart.next = reverseNext
  return prevStart
}
```

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var reverseKGroup = function(head, k) {
  let count = 0
  const myHead = new ListNode()
  let t = myHead
  const gapHead = new ListNode()
  let tGapHead
  while(head) {
    gapHead.next = head
    tGapHead = gapHead // *
    while(tGapHead.next) {
      tGapHead = tGapHead.next
      count++
      head = head.next
      if(count % k === 0) {
        tGapHead.next = null
        while(t.next) t = t.next
        t.next = reverse(gapHead.next) // *
        break // *
      }
    }
    if(count % k !== 0) {
      while(t.next) t = t.next
      t.next = gapHead.next
    }
  }
  return myHead.next
};

function reverse(head) {
  const myHead = new ListNode()
  while(head) {
    const prev = myHead.next
    myHead.next = head
    head = head.next
    myHead.next.next = prev
  }
  return myHead.next
}
```

## âœ” 26 åˆ é™¤æœ‰åºæ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„é‡å¤é¡¹ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/remove-duplicates-from-sorted-array/)

```js
var removeDuplicates = function(nums) {
  if(!nums.length) return 0
  let count = 1
  for(let i = 1; i < nums.length; i++) {
    if(nums[i] !== nums[i - 1]) {
      nums[count] = nums[i]
      count++
    }
  }
  return count 
};
```

## âœ” 27 ç§»é™¤å…ƒç´ ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/remove-element/)

```js
var removeElement = function(nums, val) {
  const len = nums.length
  let index = 0
  for(let i=0;i<len;i++) {
    if(nums[i] !== val) {
      nums[index++] = nums[i]
    }
  }
  return index
};
```

## âœ” 28 å®ç° strStr()ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/implement-strstr/)

```js
// M=haystack.length N=needle.length
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(M*N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var strStr = function(haystack, needle) {
  if(!needle.length) return 0
  for(let i=0;i<haystack.length;i++) {
    if(haystack[i] === needle[0]) {
      let j=1
      for(;j<needle.length;j++) {
        if(i + j >= haystack.length || needle[j] !== haystack[i + j]) break
      }
      if(j === needle.length) return i
    }
  }
  return -1
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 31 ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªæ’åˆ—ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/next-permutation/)

```js
var nextPermutation = function(nums) {
  const len = nums.length
  let i = len - 1
  for(;i>0;i--) {
    if(nums[i] > nums[i - 1]) {
      break
    }
  }
  for(let j = len - 1;j >= i ;j--) {
    if(nums[j] > nums[i - 1]) {
      swap(nums, i - 1, j)
      break
    }
  }
  reverse(nums, i, len - 1)
  return nums
};

function swap(arr, i, j) {
  const t = arr[i]
  arr[i] = arr[j]
  arr[j] = t
}

function reverse(arr, l, r) {
  const mid = Math.floor((l + r) / 2)
  for(let i=l;i<=mid;i++) {
    const t = arr[i]
    arr[i] = arr[r + l - i]
    arr[r + l - i] = t
  }
}
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 32 æœ€é•¿æœ‰æ•ˆæ‹¬å·ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/longest-valid-parentheses/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
var longestValidParentheses = function(s) {
  const len = s.length
  const dp = new Array(len).fill(0)
  dp[0] = 0
  for(let i=1;i<len;i++) {
    if(s[i] === ')') {
      if(s[i - 1] === '(') {
        dp[i] = (i - 2 >= 0?dp[i - 2] : 0) + 2
      } else if(i - 1 - dp[i - 1] >=0 && s[i - 1 - dp[i - 1]] === '(') {
        dp[i] = 2 + dp[i - 1] + (i - 2 - dp[i - 1] >=0 ? dp[i - 2 - dp[i - 1]] : 0) 
      }
    }
  }
  return Math.max(...dp)
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 33 æœç´¢æ—‹è½¬æ’åºæ•°ç»„ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/search-in-rotated-sorted-array/)

![](https://qiniu1.lxfriday.xyz/feoffer/1653007574423_685e61d8-c663-4699-8719-3b7d78a01427.png)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(logn)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
var search = function(nums, target) {
  const len = nums.length
  if(!len) return -1
  if(len === 1) return target === nums[0] ? 0 : -1
  let l = 0
  let r = len - 1
  while(l <= r) {
    const mid = Math.floor((l + r) / 2)
    if(target === nums[mid]) {
      return mid
    }
    if(nums[0] <= nums[mid]) {
      if(nums[0] <= target && target < nums[mid]) {
        r= mid - 1
      } else {
        l = mid + 1
      }
    } else {
      if(nums[mid] < target && target <= nums[r]) {
        l = mid + 1
      } else {
        r = mid - 1
      }
    }
  }
  return  -1
};

```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 34 åœ¨æ’åºæ•°ç»„ä¸­æŸ¥æ‰¾å…ƒç´ çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå’Œæœ€åä¸€ä¸ªä½ç½®ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/find-first-and-last-position-of-element-in-sorted-array/)

äºŒåˆ†æœç´¢

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(logn)
// ç©ºå¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var searchRange = function(nums, target) {
  const leftIndex = binarySearch(nums, target, true)
  const rightIndex = binarySearch(nums, target, false) - 1
  if(
    leftIndex >= 0 &&
    rightIndex < nums.length &&
    nums[leftIndex] === target &&
    nums[rightIndex] === target
  ) {
    return [leftIndex, rightIndex]
  }
  
  return [-1, -1]
};

function binarySearch(nums, target, lower) {
  const len = nums.length
  let l = 0
  let r = len - 1
  let resIndex = len
  while(l <= r) {
    const mid = Math.floor((l + r) / 2)
    if(target < nums[mid] || (lower && target <= nums[mid])) {
      r = mid - 1
      resIndex = mid
    } else {
      l = mid + 1
    }
  }
  return resIndex
}
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 37 è§£æ•°ç‹¬ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/sudoku-solver/)

åŒ[#51 Nçš‡å](https://leetcode.cn/problems/n-queens/)é—®é¢˜æ¯”è¾ƒç±»ä¼¼

å›æº¯ã€æšä¸¾

```js
// åŸºæœ¬ä¸Šåªè¦æ˜¯æ¶‰åŠåˆ°æšä¸¾çš„ï¼Œéƒ½å¯ä»¥ç”¨ä¸‹é¢çš„è¿™ç§æ–¹å¼ï¼Œè§£æ³•åŒæ ·é€‚ç”¨äº N çš‡åé—®é¢˜
// å…ˆæ‰«æçŸ©é˜µï¼ŒæŠŠçŸ©é˜µä¸­çš„æ•°å­—å¡«å……åˆ°å…¶å¯¹åº”çš„è¡Œã€åˆ—ã€3x3 å®«æ ¼ä¸­ï¼Œç”¨äºåç»­å¡«å……æ•°å­—æ—¶çš„å†²çªæ£€æµ‹
// åé¢ç”¨ dfs æšä¸¾æ¯ä¸ªç©ºæ ¼å¤„èƒ½å¡«å……çš„æ•°å­—ï¼Œä¸” dfs ä¼šè¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªå¸ƒå°”å€¼
// è¡¨ç¤ºå½“å‰ä½ç½®å¡«å……å¯¹åº”æ•°å­—ä¹‹ååç»­ dfs èƒ½å¦æˆåŠŸæŠŠä¹å®«æ ¼å¡«æ»¡ï¼Œè¿”å› true å°±è¡¨ç¤ºå¡«æ»¡äº†ï¼Œé‚£å°±ç›´æ¥ä¹Ÿè¿”å› true
// è¿™é¢˜éœ€è¦ç”¨åŸåœ°ä¿®æ”¹çš„å¤„ç†æ–¹å¼ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ç›´æ¥ return ç”¨æ¥é˜»æ–­åç»­çš„æšä¸¾
// å¦å¤–æˆ‘ä½¿ç”¨äº† matrixIndex æ¥è¡¨ç¤ºä¹å®«æ ¼æ ¼ä¸­å¯¹åº”çš„ä½ç½®ï¼Œè¿™æ ·å¯ä»¥é¿å… i æˆ–è€… j åˆ°å¤´ä¹‹åéš¾ä»¥æ‰¾åˆ°ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ª i j çš„é—®é¢˜
// matrixIndex èƒ½ç›´æ¥æ¨æ–­å‡º i jï¼Œè€Œ matrixIndex æœ€å¤§ä¸º n ** 2 - 1 = 80
var solveSudoku = function(board) {
  const rows = new Array(9).fill(0).map(_ => new Set())
  const cols = new Array(9).fill(0).map(_ => new Set())
  const blocks = new Array(9).fill(0).map(_ => new Set())

  for(let i=0;i<9;i++) {
    for(let j=0;j<9;j++) {
      if(board[i][j] !== '.') {
        rows[i].add(board[i][j])
        cols[j].add(board[i][j])
        blocks[Math.floor(i / 3) * 3 + Math.floor(j / 3)].add(board[i][j])
      }
    }
  }

  function dfs(matrixIndex) {
    let i = Math.floor(matrixIndex / 9)
    let j = matrixIndex - i * 9
    while(matrixIndex < 81 && board[i][j] !== '.') {
      matrixIndex ++
      i = Math.floor(matrixIndex / 9)
      j = matrixIndex - i * 9
    }

    if(matrixIndex === 81) {
      return true
    } else {
      for(let num = 1;num<=9;num++) {
        const numStr = String(num)
        const blockIndex = Math.floor(i / 3) * 3 + Math.floor(j / 3)
        if(
          !rows[i].has(numStr) &&
          !cols[j].has(numStr) &&
          !blocks[blockIndex].has(numStr)
        ) {
          board[i][j] = numStr
          rows[i].add(numStr)
          cols[j].add(numStr)
          blocks[blockIndex].add(numStr)

          if(dfs(matrixIndex + 1)) {
            return true
          } else {
            board[i][j] = '.'
            rows[i].delete(numStr)
            cols[j].delete(numStr)
            blocks[blockIndex].delete(numStr)
          }
        }
      }
      return false
    }
  }

  dfs(0)
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 38. å¤–è§‚æ•°åˆ—ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/count-and-say/)

å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€æ¨¡æ‹Ÿ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N*M) M ä¸ºç”Ÿæˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„æœ€å¤§é•¿åº¦
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var countAndSay = function(n) {
  let numStr = '1'
  n--
  while(n > 0) {
    let tStr = ''
    let l=0
    while(l < numStr.length) {
      let r = l + 1
      while(r < numStr.length && numStr[r] === numStr[l]) {
        r++
      }
      tStr += (r-l) + numStr[l]
      l=r
    }
    numStr = tStr
    n--
  }
  return numStr
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 39. ç»„åˆæ€»å’Œã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/combination-sum/)

å›æº¯æ³•ã€æ’åˆ—ç»„åˆ

```js
var combinationSum = function(candidates, target) {
  const res = []
  function walk(path, sum, startIndex) {
    if(sum === target) {
      res.push([...path])
    }
    for(let i=startIndex;i<candidates.length;i++) {
      if(sum + candidates[i] <= target) {
        path.push(candidates[i])
        walk(path, sum + candidates[i], i)
        path.pop()
      }
    }
  }
  walk([], 0, 0)
  return res
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 40. ç»„åˆæ€»å’Œ IIã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/combination-sum-ii/)

å›æº¯æ³•ã€æ’åˆ—ç»„åˆ

```js
var combinationSum2 = function(candidates, target) {
  const res = []
  candidates.sort((a, b) => a - b)
  const used = new Array(candidates.length).fill(false)
  function walk(path, sum, startIndex) {
    if(sum === target) {
      res.push([...path])
      return
    }
    for(let i=startIndex;i<candidates.length;i++) {
      if(i - 1 >= startIndex && !used[i - 1] && candidates[i] === candidates[i - 1]) continue
      if(sum + candidates[i] <= target) {
        path.push(candidates[i])
        used[i] = true
        walk(path, sum + candidates[i], i + 1)
        path.pop()
        used[i] = false
      }
    }
  }
  walk([], 0, 0)
  return res
};

```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 41 ç¼ºå¤±çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæ­£æ•°ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/first-missing-positive/)

æ•°ç»„ã€å“ˆå¸Œ

```js
// åŸåœ°å“ˆå¸Œå°±ç›¸å½“äºï¼Œè®©æ¯ä¸ªæ•°å­—néƒ½å›åˆ°ä¸‹æ ‡ä¸ºn-1çš„å®¶é‡Œã€‚
// è€Œé‚£äº›æ²¡æœ‰å›åˆ°å®¶é‡Œçš„å°±æˆäº†å­¤é­‚é‡é¬¼æµæµªåœ¨å¤–ï¼Œä»–ä»¬è¦ä¹ˆæ˜¯æ ¹æœ¬å°±æ²¡æœ‰è‡ªå·±çš„å®¶ï¼ˆæ•°å­—å°äºç­‰äº0æˆ–è€…å¤§äºnums.size()ï¼‰ï¼Œè¦ä¹ˆæ˜¯è‡ªå·±çš„å®¶è¢«åˆ«äººå é¢†äº†ï¼ˆå‡ºç°äº†é‡å¤ï¼‰ã€‚
// è¿™äº›æµæµªæ±‰è¢«ä¸´æ—¶å®‰ç½®åœ¨ä¸‹æ ‡ä¸ºiçš„ç©ºæˆ¿å­é‡Œï¼Œä¹‹æ‰€ä»¥æœ‰ç©ºæˆ¿å­æ˜¯å› ä¸ºæˆ¿å­içš„ä¸»äººi+1å¤±è¸ªäº†ï¼ˆæ•°å­—i+1ç¼ºå¤±ï¼‰ã€‚
// å› æ­¤é€šè¿‡åŸåœ°æ„å»ºå“ˆå¸Œè®©å„ä¸ªæ•°å­—å›å®¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°±å¯ä»¥æ‰¾åˆ°åŸå§‹æ•°ç»„ä¸­é‡å¤çš„æ•°å­—è¿˜æœ‰æ¶ˆå¤±çš„æ•°å­—ã€‚
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var firstMissingPositive = function(nums) {
 const len = nums.length
 for(let i=0;i<len;i++) {
   while(nums[i] - 1 >= 0 && nums[i] - 1 < len && nums[nums[i] - 1] !== nums[i]) {
     swap(nums, i, nums[i] - 1)
   }
 }
 for(let i=0;i<len;i++) {
   if(i + 1 !== nums[i]) {
     return i + 1
   }
 }
 return len + 1
};

function swap(arr, i, j) {
  const t = arr[i]
  arr[i] = arr[j]
  arr[j] = t
}
```


```js
// å¸¸è§„æ€è·¯
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
var firstMissingPositive = function(nums) {
  const s = new Set(nums)
  let i=1
  while(true) {
    if(!s.has(i)) return i
    i++
  }
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 42 æ¥é›¨æ°´ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/trapping-rain-water/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

åŒæŒ‡é’ˆç‰ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var trap = function(height) {
  let lMax = 0
  let rMax = 0
  let l = 0
  let r = height.length - 1
  let total = 0
  while(l < r) {
    if(height[l] < height[r]) {
      lMax = Math.max(lMax, height[l])
      total += lMax - height[l]
      l ++
    } else {
      rMax = Math.max(rMax, height[r])
      total += rMax - height[r]
      r--
    }
  }
  return total
};
```

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’ç‰ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
var trap = function(height) {
  const len = height.length
  const leftMax = [0]
  const rightMax = []
  rightMax[len - 1] = [0]
  let total = 0
  for(let i = 1; i < len; i++) {
    leftMax[i] = Math.max(height[i - 1], leftMax[i - 1])
  }
  for(let i = len - 2; i >= 0; i--) {
    rightMax[i] = Math.max(height[i + 1], rightMax[i + 1])
  }
  for(let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    total += Math.max(Math.min(leftMax[i], rightMax[i]) - height[i], 0)
  }

  return total
};
```

å¸¸è§„æ€è·¯ç‰ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var trap = function(height) {
  const len = height.length
  let total = 0
  for(let i = 1; i < len - 1; i++) {
    let l = i - 1
    let r = i + 1
    let lMax = height[i]
    let rMax = height[i]

    while(l >= 0) {
      if(height[l] > lMax) {
        lMax = height[l]
      } 
      l--
    }
    while(r <= len - 1) {
      if(height[r] > rMax) {
        rMax = height[r]
      } 
      r++
    }
    const receive = Math.min(lMax, rMax) - height[i]
    total += receive
  }
  return total
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 43 å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç›¸ä¹˜ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/multiply-strings/)

å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç›¸åŠ ã€å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç›¸ä¹˜

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(MN)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(M+N)
var multiply = function(num1, num2) {
  if(num1 === '0' || num2 === '0') return '0'
  const dp = new Array(num1.length + num2.length).fill(0)
  for(let i=num1.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    for(let j=num2.length - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
      let k = i + j + 1
      dp[k] += num1[i] * num2[j]
      while(dp[k] > 9) {
        dp[k-1] += Math.floor(dp[k] / 10)
        dp[k] = dp[k] % 10
        k--
      }
    }
  }
  while(dp[0] === 0) dp.shift()
  return dp.join('')
};
```

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(mn)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m + n)
var multiply = function(num1, num2) {
  if(num1 === '0' || num2 === '0') return '0'
  const m = num1.length
  const n = num2.length
  const numArr = new Array(m + n).fill(0)
  for(let i=m - 1;i>=0;i--) {
    for(let j=n - 1;j>=0;j--) {
      let addIndex = i + j + 1
      const sum = Number(num1[i]) * Number(num2[j]) + numArr[addIndex]
      numArr[addIndex] = sum % 10
      k = Math.floor(sum / 10)
      while(k > 0) {
        addIndex--
        const s = k + numArr[addIndex]
        numArr[addIndex] = s % 10
        k = Math.floor(s / 10)
      }
    }
  }
  while(numArr[0] === 0) numArr.shift()
  return numArr.join('')
};
```

or

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(mn + n^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m + n) ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦å–å†³äº sum è¿™ä¸ªå­˜å‚¨ä¸­é—´çŠ¶æ€çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²é•¿åº¦ï¼Œå®é™…ä¸Šä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥è®¤ä¸ºæ˜¯ O(1)
var multiply = function(num1, num2) {
  if(num1 === '0' || num2 === '0') return "0"
  const len1 = num1.length
  let sum = '0'
  for(let i=len1 -1;i>=0;i--) {
    const target = num1[i]
    sum = stringAdd(smallMulti(target, num2, len1 - i - 1), sum)
  }
  return sum
};

// å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç›¸ä¹˜ï¼Œxåªæœ‰ä¸€ä½
// zeroCount æ˜¯åç½®0çš„ä¸ªæ•°
function smallMulti(x, y, zeroCount) {
  if(x === '0') return '0'
  const yLen = y.length
  let add = 0
  let res = ''
  
  for(let i=yLen - 1;i>=0;i--) {
    const n = Number(x) * Number(y[i]) + add
    add = Math.floor(n / 10)
    res = (n - add * 10) + res
  }
  if(add > 0) {
    res = add + res
  }
  let zeros = ''
  for(let i=0;i<zeroCount;i++) {
    zeros +='0'
  }
  return res + zeros
}

// ä»»æ„æ•°å­—å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç›¸åŠ 
function stringAdd(x, y) {
  const xLen = x.length
  const yLen = y.length
  if(xLen >= yLen) {
    for(let i=0;i<xLen - yLen;i++) {
      y = '0' + y
    }
  } else {
    for(let i=0;i<yLen - xLen;i++) {
      x = '0' + x
    }
  }
  let res = ''
  let add = 0
  for(let i=x.length - 1;i>=0;i--) {
    const sum = Number(x[i]) + Number(y[i]) + add
    add = Math.floor(sum / 10)
    res = (sum - add * 10) + res
  }
  if(add > 0) {
    res = add + res
  }
  return res
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 45 è·³è·ƒæ¸¸æˆ IIã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/jump-game-ii/)

è´ªå¿ƒç®—æ³•

```js
// ä»åå¾€å‰åˆ†æï¼Œè´ªå¿ƒçš„æ‰¾åˆ°èƒ½åˆ°è¾¾æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—çš„æœ€è¿œæ•°å­—
// å¯èƒ½ä¼šæ‹…å¿ƒåˆ°ä¸äº†è¿™ä¸ªä¸‹æ ‡ï¼Œå®é™…ä¸Šï¼Œå¦‚æœåˆ°ä¸äº†è¿™ä¸ªä¸‹æ ‡ï¼Œåˆ™ä¸€å®šåˆ°ä¸äº†æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªä¸‹æ ‡ï¼Œæ•…è¿™ä¸ªä¸‹æ ‡æ˜¯ä¸€å®šèƒ½åˆ°çš„
// ç”¨ç›¸åŒçš„åŠæ³•ï¼Œä¸æ–­åœ°æŠŠä¸‹æ ‡ä»¥æ¯æ¬¡æœ€è¿œçš„è·ç¦»å¾€å‰é è¿‘ï¼Œç›´åˆ°åˆ°è¾¾ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var jump = function(nums) {
  let r = nums.length - 1
  let min = 0
  while(r > 0) {
    for(let i = 0; i < r; i++) {
      if(i + nums[i] >= r) {
        r = i
        min++
        break
      }
    }
  }
  return min
};
```

æ›´ä¼˜ç‰ˆæœ¬

ä¸å¤ªå¥½ç†è§£ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å‚ç…§è¿™å¼ å›¾ï¼Œé»‘è‰²çš„è¹¦è·¶çº¿ä»£è¡¨æ¯æ¬¡è·³çš„æ—¶å€™èƒ½è·³çš„æœ€è¿œè·ç¦»ï¼Œçº¢è‰²çº¿ä»ç»ˆç‚¹åè¿‡æ¥æ¨ï¼Œåœ¨æ¯ä¸ªé»‘è‰²èµ·è·³åŒºé—´å†…æ‰¾ä¸€ä¸ªå€¼ï¼Œæœ€ç»ˆæ¨åˆ°èµ·è·³ç‚¹ä½äº0ã€‚

![](https://qiniu1.lxfriday.xyz/feoffer/1652678598702_5db9138d-58b3-4bbf-81ae-44b6795bacc5.png)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var jump = function(nums) {
  // æ¯ç§»åŠ¨ä¸€æ¬¡ä¸‹æ ‡éƒ½è®¡ç®—ä¸€æ¬¡èƒ½èµ°åˆ°çš„æœ€è¿œè·ç¦»
  let maxIndex1 = 0
  // å½“èµ°åˆ°ä¸Šä¸€è½®èƒ½èµ°åˆ°çš„æœ€è¿œä¸‹æ ‡çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œæ›´æ–°å½“å‰è½®æ¬¡èƒ½èµ°çš„æœ€è¿œä¸‹æ ‡
  let maxIndex2 = 0
  let count = 0
  for(let i = 0; i < nums.length - 1; i++) {
    maxIndex1 = Math.max(maxIndex1, i + nums[i])
    if(i === maxIndex2) {
      count++
      maxIndex2 = maxIndex1
    }
  }
  return count
};
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 46 å…¨æ’åˆ—ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/permutations/)

æ’åˆ—ç»„åˆã€å›æº¯æ³•ã€é€’å½’

```js
var permute = function(nums) {
  const numsLen = nums.length
  const res = []
  const used = {}
  function dfs(path) {
    if(path.length === numsLen) {
      res.push([...path])
      return
    }
    for(let i = 0; i < numsLen; i++){
      const num = nums[i]
      if(used[i]) continue
      used[i] = true
      dfs([...path, num])
      used[i] = false
    }
  }

  dfs([])
  return res
};
```
or

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n!)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n) é€’å½’çš„å±‚æ•°
var permute = function(nums) {
  const res = []

  function calc(path) {
    if(path.length === nums.length) {
      res.push(path)
      return
    }
    nums.forEach(n => {
      if(!path.includes(n)) {
        calc([...path, n])
      }
    })
  }
  calc([])
  return res
};
```

or

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n!)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
var permute = function(nums) {
  if(nums.length === 1) return [nums]
  const res = []
  for(let i = 0;i < nums.length; i++) {
    permute(nums.slice(0, i).concat(nums.slice(i + 1))).forEach(_ => {
      res.push([nums[i], ..._])
    })
  }
  return res
};
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 47 å…¨æ’åˆ— IIã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/permutations-ii/)

æ’åˆ—ç»„åˆã€å›æº¯æ³•ã€é€’å½’

æ— æ’åº

```js
var permuteUnique = function(nums) {
  const n = nums.length
  const res = []
  const used = new Array(n).fill(false)
  function walk(path) {
    if(path.length === n) {
      res.push([...path])
      return
    }
    const levelUsed = new Set()
    for(let i=0;i<n;i++) {
      if(levelUsed.has(nums[i]) || used[i]) continue
      levelUsed.add(nums[i])
      used[i] = true
      path.push(nums[i])
      walk(path)
      used[i] = false
      path.pop()
    }
  }
  walk([])
  return res
};
```

æ’åº
```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n*n!)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
var permuteUnique = function(nums) {
  // æŠŠæ— åºæ•°ç»„æ’æˆæœ‰åºçš„ï¼Œæ–¹ä¾¿åé¢ç›¸åŒæ•°å­—çš„å¤„ç†
  nums.sort((a, b) => a - b)
  const numsLen = nums.length
  const res = []
  // å¯¹æŸä¸ªå€¼æ˜¯å¦ä½¿ç”¨è¿‡åšä¸€ä¸ªè®°å½•
  const used = {}
  function dfs(path) {
    if(path.length === numsLen) {
      res.push([...path])
      return
    }
    for(let i = 0; i < numsLen; i++){
      const num = nums[i]
      // åœ¨ç›¸åŒå±‚çº§çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œå¦‚æœåç»­è¿˜æœ‰å¾ˆå¤šç›¸åŒçš„æ•°å­—ï¼Œåˆ™éƒ½ä¼šç›´æ¥è·³è¿‡
      // è€Œè¿™é‡Œ num === nums[i - 1] å°±æ˜¯è¡¨ç¤ºç›¸åŒçš„æ•°å­—
      // !used[i - 1] è¡¨ç¤ºçš„æ˜¯ç›¸åŒå±‚çº§ï¼Œå³æ•°ç»„ä¸­è£…å¡«çš„æ•°å­—ä¸ªæ•°ç›¸åŒå°±è¡¨ç¤ºæ˜¯åŒä¸€å±‚çº§
      if(used[i] || (i >= 1 && num === nums[i - 1] && !used[i - 1])) continue
      used[i] = true
      path.push(num)
      // è¿™ä¸ªåœ°æ–¹åœ¨ dfs å‰åä¼šæŠŠ used[i] çš„å€¼æ›´æ”¹ä¸¤æ¬¡
      // åŸå› æ˜¯ï¼šæ‰§è¡Œ dfs å‰ï¼Œç½®ä¸º trueï¼Œç„¶åè¿›è¡Œ dfs å†…çš„é€’å½’è°ƒç”¨æ—¶ï¼Œè¯¥è°ƒç”¨æ ˆå†…éƒ½ä¼šå¾—åˆ° used[i] ä¸º true
      dfs(path)
      path.pop()
      used[i] = false
    }
  }

  dfs([])
  return res
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 48. æ—‹è½¬å›¾åƒã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/rotate-image/)

æ•°ç»„ã€æ—‹è½¬æ•°ç»„ã€çŸ©é˜µ

```js
// åŸåœ°ç½®æ¢
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var rotate = function(matrix) {
  const n = matrix.length;
  for (let i = 0; i < Math.floor(n / 2); ++i) {
    for (let j = 0; j < Math.floor((n + 1) / 2); ++j) {
      const temp = matrix[i][j];
      matrix[i][j] = matrix[n - j - 1][i];
      matrix[n - j - 1][i] = matrix[n - i - 1][n - j - 1];
      matrix[n - i - 1][n - j - 1] = matrix[j][n - i - 1];
      matrix[j][n - i - 1] = temp;
    }
  }
};
```

```js
// å¸¸è§„è§£æ³•
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N^2)
var rotate = function(matrix) {
  const n = matrix.length
  const tmpArr = new Array(n).fill([]).map(_ => [])
  for(let i = 0;i < n;i++) {
    for(let j = 0;j< n;j++) {
      tmpArr[j][n - 1 - i] = matrix[i][j]
    }
  }
  for(let i = 0;i < n;i++) {
    for(let j = 0;j< n;j++) {
      matrix[i][j] = tmpArr[i][j]
    }
  }
};
// 0 3 => 3 3
// 0 2 => 2 3
// 1 1 => 1 2
// 2 1 => 1 1
// 3 0 => 0 0
```

## âœ” 49 å­—æ¯å¼‚ä½è¯åˆ†ç»„ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/group-anagrams/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(NKlogK)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(NK)
var groupAnagrams = function(strs) {
  const map = new Map()
  for(let i=0;i<strs.length;i++) {
    const hash = strs[i].split('').sort((a, b) => a.charCodeAt(0) - b.charCodeAt(0)).join('')
    map.set(hash,map.has(hash) ? [...map.get(hash), strs[i]]: [strs[i]])
  }
  return Array.from(map.values())
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 51 N çš‡åã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/n-queens/)

å›æº¯ã€æšä¸¾

```js
var solveNQueens = function(n) {
  const rows = new Set()
  const cols = new Set()
  // å¯¹ç§°è½´å·¦ä¸Š
  const leftTop = new Set()
  // å¯¹ç§°è½´å³ä¸Š
  const rightTop = new Set()
  const preRes = []

  function dfs(matrixIndex, path, k) {
    if(k === 0) {
      preRes.push([...path])
      return
    }
    if(matrixIndex >= n ** 2) {
      return
    }

    let i = Math.floor(matrixIndex / n)
    let j = matrixIndex - i * n
    if(
      !rows.has(i) &&
      !cols.has(j) &&
      !leftTop.has(i + j) &&
      !rightTop.has(j - i)
    ) {
      path.push(matrixIndex)
      rows.add(i)
      cols.add(j)
      leftTop.add(i + j)
      rightTop.add(j - i)

      dfs(matrixIndex + 1, path, k - 1)

      path.pop()
      rows.delete(i)
      cols.delete(j)
      leftTop.delete(i + j)
      rightTop.delete(j - i)
    }
    dfs(matrixIndex + 1, path, k)
  }

  dfs(0, [],  n)
  const res = []
  preRes.forEach(_ => {
    const tplArr = new Array(n).fill(0).map(_ => new Array(n).fill('.'))
    for(let ind of _) {
      let i = Math.floor(ind / n)
      let j = ind - i * n
      tplArr[i][j] = 'Q'
    }
    res.push(tplArr.map(__ => __.join('')))
  })
  return res
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 53 æœ€å¤§å­æ•°ç»„å’Œã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/maximum-subarray/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

æ•°ç»„ç‰ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
var maxSubArray = function(nums) {
 const dp = []
 // dp[i] å®šä¹‰çš„æ˜¯ä»¥ i ä½œä¸ºç»“æŸçš„è¿ç»­å­æ•°ç»„çš„ æœ€å¤§å€¼
 // åˆ™æ•´ä¸ªæ•°ç»„çš„æœ€å¤§è¿ç»­å­æ•°ç»„å¿…ç„¶ä¼šå‘½ä¸­ dp ä¸­çš„ä¸€é¡¹ï¼Œä¸”ä¸ºå€¼æœ€å¤§çš„é‚£ä¸€é¡¹
 dp[0] = nums[0]
 for(let i = 1;i<nums.length;i++) {
   if(dp[i - 1] < 0) {
     dp[i] = nums[i]
   } else {
     dp[i] = dp[i - 1] + nums[i]
   }
 }
 return Math.max(...dp)
};
```

ç²¾ç®€ç‰ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
// è¿™ä¸ªè§£æ³•ç›¸æ¯”æ•°ç»„è§£æ³•æ›´éš¾ç†è§£
var maxSubArray = function(nums) {
 // å‰ i ä¸ªæ•°å­—ä¸­è¿ç»­å­æ•°ç»„çš„æœ€å¤§å’Œ
 let max = nums[0]
 // ä»¥ i ä¸ºç»“å°¾çš„è¿ç»­å­æ•°ç»„çš„æœ€å¤§å’Œ
 let sum = 0
 for(let i = 0; i < nums.length; i++) {
   if(sum < 0) {
     sum = nums[i]
   } else {
     sum = sum + nums[i]
   }
   max = Math.max(max, sum)
 }
 return max
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 54 èºæ—‹çŸ©é˜µã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/spiral-matrix/)

```js
// ç›´æ¥é€’å½’ç¡¬æ‰¾ï¼Œå¥½ç†è§£
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
var spiralOrder = function(matrix) {
  const m = matrix.length
  const n = matrix[0].length
  const used = new Array(m).fill(false).map(_ => new Array(n).fill(false))
  const res = []

  function walk(i, j, direction) {
    used[i][j] = true
    res.push(matrix[i][j])

    if(direction === 'right') {
      if((j + 1 < n) && !used[i][j + 1]) {
        walk(i, j + 1, 'right')
      } else {
        (i + 1 < m) && !used[i + 1][j] && walk(i + 1, j, 'bottom')
      }
    }

    if(direction === 'bottom') {
      if((i + 1 < m) && !used[i + 1][j]) {
        walk(i + 1, j, 'bottom')
      } else {
        (j - 1 >= 0) && !used[i][j - 1] && walk(i, j - 1, 'left')
      }
    }

    if(direction === 'left') {
      if((j - 1 >= 0) && !used[i][j - 1]) {
        walk(i, j - 1, 'left')
      } else {
        (i - 1 >= 0) && !used[i-1][j] && walk(i-1, j, 'top')
      }
    }

    if(direction === 'top') {
      if((i - 1 >= 0) && !used[i - 1][j]) {
        walk(i - 1, j, 'top')
      } else {
        (j + 1 < n) && !used[i][j + 1] && walk(i, j + 1, 'right')
      }
    }
  }

  walk(0, 0, 'right')

  return res
};
```


## ğŸ˜»âœ” 55 è·³è·ƒæ¸¸æˆã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/jump-game/)

```js
// ä»å·¦å¾€å³æ‰«æ i ä½ç½®å¾€åæœ€å¤šèƒ½è·³åˆ°å“ª
// maxIndex ç”¨æ¥è®°å½• i å‰é¢æœ€å¤šèƒ½è·³åˆ°å“ªä¸ªä¸‹æ ‡ï¼Œæ¯åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªä½ç½®éƒ½åˆ·æ–° maxIndex
// å¦‚æœå‡ºç° maxIndex < iï¼Œåˆ™è¯´æ˜iå‰é¢çš„ä½ç½®æ— æ³•è·³åˆ° i
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var canJump = function(nums) {
  let maxIndex = 0
  for(let i = 0; i < nums.length; i++) {
    if(i > maxIndex) return false
    maxIndex = Math.max(i + nums[i], maxIndex)
  }
  return true
};
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 56 åˆå¹¶åŒºé—´ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/merge-intervals/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(NlogN) æ’åº
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(logN) æ’åº
var merge = function(intervals) {
  intervals.sort((a, b) => a[0] - b[0])
  const res = []
  while(intervals.length > 1) {
    let first = intervals.shift()
    let second = intervals.shift()
    // åŒºé—´æœ‰äº¤é›†
    if(first[1] >= second[1]) {
      second = first
    } else if(first[1] >= second[0]) {
      second = [first[0], second[1]]
    } else {
      res.push(first)
    }
    intervals.unshift(second)
  }
  res.push(intervals.shift())
  return res
};
```

## ?ğŸ˜»âœ” 60. æ’åˆ—åºåˆ—ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/permutation-sequence/)

å›æº¯æ³•ã€æ’åˆ—ç»„åˆã€è§„å¾‹é¢˜

é¢˜è§£

- [ã€äº‘å½±åŒå­¦ã€‘å›æº¯å‰ªæï¼Œç›´è¾¾ç›®æ ‡æ•°å­—](https://leetcode.cn/problems/permutation-sequence/solution/by-lxfriday-msh9/)

```js
// æœ€ç®€å•çš„è§£æ³•
var getPermutation = function(n, k) {
  let res
  const used = new Array(10).fill(false)
  function walk(path) {
    if(path.length === n) {
      res = path
      return
    }
    let cnt = 0
    const len = n - path.length
    for(let i=1;i<=n;i++) {
      if(used[i]) continue
      cnt++
      const sumCount = cnt * steps(len - 1)
      if(sumCount >= k) {
        k -= (cnt - 1) * steps(len - 1)
        used[i] = true
        walk(path + i)
        used[i] = false
        break
      }
    }
  }
  walk('')
  return res
};
function steps(n) {
  if(n === 0) return 1
  if(n === 1) return 1
  return n * steps(n - 1)
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 62 ä¸åŒè·¯å¾„ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/unique-paths/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(mn)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(mn)
var uniquePaths = function(m, n) {
  const dp = new Array(m).fill(0).map(_ => new Array(n).fill(0))
  dp[0][0] = 1
  for(let i=1;i<m;i++) {
    dp[i][0] = dp[i - 1][0]
  }
  for(let j=1;j<n;j++) {
    dp[0][j] = dp[0][j - 1]
  }
  for(let i=1;i<m;i++) {
    for(let j=1;j<n;j++) {
      dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j] + dp[i][j - 1]
    } 
  }
  return dp[m - 1][n - 1]
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 63. ä¸åŒè·¯å¾„ IIã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/unique-paths-ii/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(MN)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(MN)
var uniquePathsWithObstacles = function(grid) {
  if(grid[0][0] === 1) return 0
  const m = grid.length
  const n = grid[0].length
  const dp = new Array(m).fill(0).map(_ => new Array(n).fill(0))
  dp[0][0] = 1
  for(let i=1;i<m;i++) {
    dp[i][0] = (grid[i][0] === 0 && dp[i - 1][0] !== 0) ? 1 : 0
  }
  for(let j=1;j<n;j++) {
    dp[0][j] = (grid[0][j] === 0 && dp[0][j - 1] !== 0) ? 1 : 0
  }
  for(let i=1;i<m;i++) {
    for(let j=1;j<n;j++) {
      if(grid[i][j] === 1) {
        dp[i][j] = 0
      } else {
        dp[i][j] = dp[i-1][j] + dp[i][j - 1]
      }
    }
  }
  return dp[m-1][n-1]
};
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 64. æœ€å°è·¯å¾„å’Œã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/minimum-path-sum/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(MN)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
var minPathSum = function(grid) {
  const m = grid.length, n = grid[0].length
  let dp = new Array(n).fill(Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER)
  dp[0] = grid[0][0]
  for(let j=1;j<n;j++) {
    dp[j] = grid[0][j] + dp[j-1]
  }
  for(let i=1;i<m;i++) {
    const tdp = []
    for(let j=0;j<n;j++) {
      if(j === 0) {
        tdp.push(dp[0] + grid[i][j])
      } else {
        tdp.push(grid[i][j] + Math.min(dp[j], tdp[j-1]))
      }
    }
    dp = tdp
  }
  return dp[n-1]
};
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 65 æœ‰æ•ˆçš„æ•°å­—ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/valid-number/)

```js
var isNumber = function(s) {
  // if(s === 'Infinity' || s === '+Infinity' || s === '-Infinity') return false
  // const num = Number(s)
  // if(isNaN(num)) return false
  // return true
  // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿæ³•
  let numLeft = ''
  let numRight = ''
  s = s.trim().toLowerCase()
 if(s.includes('e')) {
    const sSplit = s.split('e')
    if(sSplit.length > 2) { return false }
    [numLeft, numRight] = sSplit
    if(validateNumLeft(numLeft) && validateNumRight(numRight)) return true
  } else {
    numLeft = s
    if(validateNumLeft(numLeft)) return true
  }
  return false
};

function validateNumLeft(numLeft) {
  if('-+'.includes(numLeft[0])) {
    numLeft = numLeft.slice(1)
    if(numLeft.includes('-') || numLeft.includes('+')) return false
  }
  if(!numLeft.length) return false
  let numLeftSplit
  if(numLeft.includes('.')) {
    numLeftSplit = numLeft.split('.')
    if(numLeftSplit.length > 2 ) return false
    if(!numLeftSplit[0].length && isNumStr(numLeftSplit[1])) return true
    if(!numLeftSplit[1].length && isNumStr(numLeftSplit[0])) return true
    if(isNumStr(numLeftSplit[0]) && isNumStr(numLeftSplit[1])) return true
    return false
  } else {
    return isNumStr(numLeft)
  }
}

function validateNumRight(numRight) {
  if(numRight[0] === '-' || numRight[0] === '+') {
    numRight = numRight.slice(1)
  }
  return isNumStr(numRight)
}

function isNumStr(numStr) {
  if(!numStr.length) return false
  for(let c of numStr) {
    if(!(c >= '0' && c <= '9')) return false
  }
  return true
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 70 çˆ¬æ¥¼æ¢¯ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/climbing-stairs/)

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var climbStairs = function(n) {
  if(n === 1) return 1
  if(n === 2) return 2
  d1 = 1
  d2 = 2
  for(let i = 3; i <= n; i++) {
    const tmpD2 = d2
    d2 = d1 + d2
    d1 = tmpD2
  }
  return d2
};
```

æ•°ç»„è§£

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
var climbStairs = function(n) {
  const d = []
  d[1] = 1
  d[2] = 2
  for(let i = 3; i <= n; i++) {
    d[i] = d[i - 1] + d[i - 2]
  }
  return d[n]
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 72 ç¼–è¾‘è·ç¦»ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/edit-distance/)

å®šä¹‰ `dp[i][j]` æ˜¯ word1 é•¿åº¦ä¸º i çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²è½¬æ¢æˆ word2 é•¿åº¦ä¸º j å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„æœ€å°‘æ“ä½œæ¬¡æ•°ã€‚åˆ™ `dp[i][j]` å¯ç”±ä¸‹é¢ä¸‰ç§æƒ…å†µå¾—åˆ°ï¼š

- `dp[i - 1][j - 1]` æ›¿æ¢æ‰ word1 ä¸­ç¬¬ i ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦
- `dp[i - 1][j]`  åˆ é™¤ word1 ä¸­ç¬¬ i ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦
- `dp[i][j - 1]`  åœ¨ word1 ä¸­ç¬¬ i ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦åé¢æ–°å¢ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦

ä¸Šé¢ä¸‰ç§æƒ…å†µçš„æœ€å°å€¼ + 1ï¼Œå°±æ˜¯ `dp[i][j]`ã€‚

æ‰€ä»¥çŠ¶æ€è½¬ç§»æ–¹ç¨‹ä¸ºï¼š

```js
dp[i][j] = Math.min(dp[i - 1][j - 1], dp[i - 1][j], dp[i][j - 1]) + 1
```

ç„¶åè®¾ç½®åˆå§‹å€¼ï¼Œ i ä¸º 0 åˆ™æœ€çŸ­æ“ä½œæ¬¡æ•°å°±æ˜¯ jï¼Œj ä¸º 0 åˆ™æœ€çŸ­æ“ä½œæ¬¡æ•°å°±æ˜¯ iã€‚


åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’

```js
// m=word1.length n=word2.length
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
var minDistance = function(word1, word2) {
  const len1 = word1.length
  const len2 = word2.length
  const dp = new Array(len1 + 1).fill(0).map(_ => new Array(len2 + 1).fill(0))
  for(let i = 0; i <= len1; i++) {
    dp[i][0] = i
  }
  for(let j = 0; j <= len2; j++) {
    dp[0][j] = j
  }
  for(let i = 1; i <= len1; i++) {
    for(let j = 1; j <= len2; j++) {
      if(word1[i - 1] === word2[j - 1]) {
        dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j - 1]
      } else {
        dp[i][j] = Math.min(dp[i - 1][j - 1], dp[i - 1][j], dp[i][j - 1]) + 1
      }
    }
  }
  return dp[len1][len2]
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 75. é¢œè‰²åˆ†ç±»ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/sort-colors/)

åŒæŒ‡é’ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var sortColors = function(nums) {
  let l = 0, r = nums.length - 1, i = 0
  while(i <= r) {
    if(nums[i] === 0) {
      swap(nums, i, l)
      i++
      l++
    } else if(nums[i] === 2) {
      swap(nums, i, r)
      r--
    } else {
      i++
    }
  }
  return nums
};

function swap(nums, i, j) {
  const t = nums[i]
  nums[i] = nums[j]
  nums[j] = t
}
```

## ğŸ˜»âœ” 76 æœ€å°è¦†ç›–å­ä¸²ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/minimum-window-substring/)

åŒæŒ‡é’ˆã€æ»‘åŠ¨çª—å£

```js
var minWindow = function(s, t) {
  const need = new Map()
  let needType = 0
  for(let c of t) {
    if(need.has(c)) {
      need.set(c, need.get(c) + 1)
    } else {
      need.set(c, 1)
      needType += 1
    }
  }

  let l = 0
  let minStr = ''
  for(let r = 0;r < s.length; r++) {
    const c = s[r]
    if(need.has(c)) {
      need.set(c, need.get(c) - 1)
      if(need.get(c) === 0) needType -= 1 
    }
    while(needType === 0) {
      if(!minStr.length || s.slice(l, r + 1).length < minStr.length) minStr = s.slice(l, r + 1)
      if(need.has(s[l])) {
        need.set(s[l], need.get(s[l]) + 1)
        if(need.get(s[l]) === 1) {
          needType += 1
        }
      }
      l++
    }
  }
  return minStr
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 77 ç»„åˆã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/combinations/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(C(n, k)) ç»„åˆæ•°
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(k)
var combine = function(n, k) {
  const res = []

  function run(path, start) {
    if(path.length === k) {
      res.push([...path])
      return
    }

    for(let i=start;i<=n;i++) {
      path.push(i)
      run(path, i + 1)
      path.pop()
    }
  }

  run([], 1)

  return res
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 78 å­é›†ã€mediumã€‘

å›æº¯ã€é€’å½’

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N*2^N)
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
var subsets = function(nums) {
  const res = []

  function calc(path, start = 0) {
    res.push(path)
    for(let i = start; i < nums.length; i++) {
      calc([...path, nums[i]], i + 1)
    }
  }

  calc([])
  return res
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 79 å•è¯æœç´¢ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/word-search/)

```js
var exist = function(board, word) {
  const m = board.length
  const n = board[0].length
  const used = new Array(m).fill(false).map(_ => new Array(n).fill(false))
  const words = word.split('')
  let has = false

  for(let i=0;i<m;i++) {
    for(let j=0;j<n;j++) {
      find(i, j, words)
    }
  }

  function find(i, j) {
    if(used[i][j]) return
    if(board[i][j] === words[0]) {
      const w = words.shift()
      used[i][j] = true

      if(!words.length) {
        has = true
        return
      }

      j + 1 < n && find(i, j + 1)
      j - 1 >= 0 && find(i, j - 1)
      i - 1 >=0 && find(i - 1, j)
      i + 1 < m && find(i + 1, j)
      words.unshift(w)
      used[i][j] = false
    }
  }

  return has
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 80. åˆ é™¤æœ‰åºæ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„é‡å¤é¡¹ IIã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/remove-duplicates-from-sorted-array-ii/)

æ•°ç»„åŸåœ°æ“ä½œ

```typescript
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
function removeDuplicates(nums: number[]): number {
  if(nums.length < 3) return nums.length
  const n = nums.length
  let k = 2
  for(let i=2;i<n;i++) {
    if(nums[i] !== nums[k - 2]) {
      nums[k++] = nums[i]
    }
  }
  return k
};
```

```typescript
// æ¯”è¾ƒå¥½ç†è§£çš„ç‰ˆæœ¬ï¼ŒåŸåœ°æ ‡è®°ï¼Œç„¶åå†æ¬¡æ‰«æ
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
function removeDuplicates(nums: number[]): number {
  if(nums.length < 3) return nums.length
  let p1 = 0
  let p2 = 1
  const n = nums.length
  for(let i=2;i<n;i++) {
    if(nums[i] === nums[p1] && nums[i] === nums[p2]) {
      nums[i] = Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER
    } else {
      p1 = p2
      p2 = i
    }
  }
  let k = 2
  for(let i=2;i<n;i++) {
    if(nums[i] !== Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER) {
      nums[k++] = nums[i]
    }
  }
  return k
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 82 åˆ é™¤æ’åºé“¾è¡¨ä¸­çš„é‡å¤å…ƒç´  IIã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/remove-duplicates-from-sorted-list-ii/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var deleteDuplicates = function(head) {
  let myHead = new ListNode()
  myHead.next = head
  let fast = myHead
  let slow = myHead
  while(fast.next && fast.next.next) {
    if(fast.next.val === fast.next.next.val) {
      fast = fast.next
    } else {
      if(fast === slow) {
        slow = slow.next
        fast = fast.next
      } else {
        slow.next = fast.next.next
        fast = slow
      }
    }
  }
  if(slow !== fast) {
    slow.next = null
  }
  return myHead.next
};
```

## âœ” 83 åˆ é™¤æ’åºé“¾è¡¨ä¸­çš„é‡å¤å…ƒç´ ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/remove-duplicates-from-sorted-list/)

é“¾è¡¨

```js
var deleteDuplicates = function (head) {
  let t = head
  while (t && t.next) {
    const tNext = t.next
    if (t.val !== tNext.val) {
      t = t.next
    } else {
      t.next = tNext.next
    }
  }
  return head
}
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 84 æŸ±çŠ¶å›¾ä¸­æœ€å¤§çš„çŸ©å½¢ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/largest-rectangle-in-histogram/)

å•è°ƒæ ˆ

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(N)
var largestRectangleArea = function(heights) {
  heights = [0, ...heights, 0]
  let max = 0
  const q = [0]
  for(let i=1;i<heights.length;i++) {
    while(heights[i] < heights[q[q.length - 1]]) {
      const h = heights[q.pop()]
      const w = i - q[q.length - 1] - 1
      max = Math.max(max, w * h)
    }
    if(heights[i] >= heights[q[q.length - 1]]) {
      q.push(i)
    }
  }
  return max
};
```

## ?ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 85 æœ€å¤§çŸ©å½¢ã€hardã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/maximal-rectangle/)

å•è°ƒæ ˆ

ç›¸å…³è¯·çœ‹ 84 é¢˜

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m*n)
var maximalRectangle = function(matrix) {
  if(!matrix.length || !matrix[0].length) return 0
  const m = matrix.length
  const n = matrix[0].length
  const left = new Array(m).fill(0).map(_ => new Array(n).fill(0))
  for(let i=0;i<m;i++) {
    for(let j=0;j<n;j++) {
      if(matrix[i][j] === '1') {
        left[i][j] = (j - 1 >= 0 ? left[i][j - 1] : 0) + 1
      }
    }
  }
  // ç»™æ¯åˆ—åŠ å‰å¯¼0å’Œåç½®0ï¼Œå…·ä½“åŸå› è¯·çœ‹
  // #84 https://leetcode.cn/problems/largest-rectangle-in-histogram/
  // å‰å¯¼0å¯ä»¥ç”¨äº w å®½åº¦è®¡ç®—æ—¶çš„å·¦è¾¹ç•Œ
  // åç½®0å¯ä»¥ç”¨äºæ¸…ç©ºqæ ˆï¼Œqæ˜¯å¿…é¡»è¦æ¸…ç©ºçš„ï¼Œå¦‚æœä¸åŠ åç½®0ï¼Œåˆ™å¯¹äºé€’å¢çš„é«˜åº¦éœ€è¦åšé¢å¤–çš„åç½®å¤„ç†
  left.unshift(new Array(n).fill(0))
  left.push(new Array(n).fill(0))
  let max = 0
  for(let j=0;j< n;j++) {
    const q = []
    for(let i=0;i<m + 2;i++) {
      while(q.length - 1 >= 0 && left[q[q.length - 1]][j] > left[i][j]) {
        const h = left[q.pop()][j]
        const w = i - q[q.length - 1] - 1
        max = Math.max(max, w * h)
      }
      q.push(i)
    }
  }
  return max
};
```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 86. åˆ†éš”é“¾è¡¨ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/partition-list/)

```js
var partition = function(head, x) {
  const head1 = new ListNode(), head2 = new ListNode()
  let tHead1 = head1, tHead2 = head2
  while(head) {
    const next = head.next
    if(head.val < x) {
      tHead1.next = head
      tHead1 = tHead1.next
    } else {
      tHead2.next = head
      tHead2 = tHead2.next
    }
    head = next
  }
  tHead1.next = head2.next
  tHead2.next = null
  return head1.next
};
```

## âœ” 88 åˆå¹¶ä¸¤ä¸ªæœ‰åºæ•°ç»„ã€easyã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/merge-sorted-array/)

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(m+n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(1)
var merge = function(nums1, m, nums2, n) {
  let mn = m + n - 1
  let mIndex = m - 1
  let nIndex = n - 1
  while(mIndex >= 0 && nIndex >= 0) {
    if(nums1[mIndex] > nums2[nIndex]) {
      nums1[mn] = nums1[mIndex]
      mIndex--
    } else {
      nums1[mn] = nums2[nIndex]
      nIndex--
    }
    mn--
  }
  // æœ‰å¯èƒ½ nums1 ä¸­çš„æ•°å­—éƒ½å¤åˆ¶å®Œäº†ï¼Œnums2 ä¸­è¿˜å­˜åœ¨æ•°å­—
  // åˆ™æŠŠ nums2 ä¸­çš„æ•°å­—éƒ½å¤åˆ¶è¿‡æ¥
  // å¦‚æœæ˜¯ nums2 æ²¡æœ‰éœ€è¦å¤åˆ¶çš„ï¼Œè€Œ nums1 æœ‰éœ€è¦å¤åˆ¶çš„ï¼Œåˆ™å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥è·³è¿‡
  while(nIndex >= 0) {
    nums1[nIndex] = nums2[nIndex]
    nIndex--
    mn--
  }
};
```

## ?? ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 89 æ ¼é›·ç¼–ç ã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/gray-code/)

```js
// è§„å¾‹é¢˜
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(2^N)
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(2^N)
// æ³¨æ„æ¡ä»¶ï¼š
// ç»“æœæ•°ç»„ä¸­æœ‰ 2^N ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œä¸”åˆšå¥½æ˜¯ [0, 2^N -1] å†…çš„æ•°
// 1. å¯¹äº N-1 çš„æ ¼é›·ç¼–ç ï¼ŒN ä¸­çš„æ•°å­—æ˜¯N-1ä¸­æ•°å­—çš„ä¸€å€
// 2. N-1 ä¸­å·²å½¢æˆæ ¼é›·ç¼–ç çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œå¯¹è¿™ N-1 ä¸ªæ•°å­—çš„äºŒè¿›åˆ¶å‰é¢åŠ ä¸€ä¸ª1ï¼Œç„¶åç¿»è½¬å°±æ˜¯å¦å¤– 2^(N-1) ä¸ªæ•°å­—
// 0 01 => 0 01 0 01 => 0 01 10 11 => 0 01 11 10
// 0 01 11 10 => 0 01 11 10 0 01 11 10 => 0 01 11 10 100 101 111 110 => 0 01 11 10 110 111 101 100
var grayCode = function(n) {
  const res = [0];
  for (let i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
    const len = res.length;
    for (let j = len - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
      res.push(res[j] + len)
    }
  }
  return res;
};

// 0 1 11 10
// 0 1 3 2

// 0  0
// 1  1
// 2  10
// 3  11 
// 4  100
// 5  101
// 6  110
// 7  111
// 8  1000
// 9  1001
// 10 1010
// 11 1011
// 12 1100
// 13 1101
// 14 1110
// 15 1111

```

## ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 90 å­é›† IIã€mediumã€‘

[ref](https://leetcode.cn/problems/subsets-ii/)

å›æº¯ã€æ·±åº¦ä¼˜å…ˆéå†

```js
// æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(nÃ—2^n)
// ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼šO(n)
var subsetsWithDup = function(nums) {
  nums.sort((a, b) => a - b)
  const res = []
  const len = nums.length
  const used = []
  function dfs(path, index) {
    res.push(path)
    for(let i=index;i<len;i++) {
      if(i - 1 >= index && !used[i - 1] && nums[i] === nums[i - 1]) continue
      used[i] = true
      dfs([...path, nums[i]], i + 1)
      used[i] = false
    }
  }
  dfs([], 0)
  return res
};
```

## ?? ğŸŒŸğŸ˜»âœ” 91. è§£ç æ–¹æ³•ã€mediumã€‘

```js
var numDecodings = function(s) {
  if(s[0] === '0') return 0
  const n = s.length
  let v1 = 0, v2 = 1
  for(let i = 1; i < n; i++) {
    if(s[i] === '0' && s[i - 1] !== '1' && s[i - 1] !== '2') return 0

      nextV2 += (i - 2 >= 0 ? pv1 : 1)
    }
    v1 = pv2
    v2 = nextV2
  }
  return v2
};
```
